			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">2011 IIHF World Championship rosters</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div role="note" class="hatnote">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2011_IIHF_World_Championship" title="2011 IIHF World Championship">2011 IIHF World Championship</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="An ice hockey player standing in the goals with his body turned to the right of the camera. He is wearing a black and white uniform." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg/200px-Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg" width="200" height="267" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg/300px-Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg/400px-Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2319" data-file-height="3092" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Fasth_Viktor_AIK_2011_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Viktor_Fasth" title="Viktor Fasth">Viktor Fasth</a> of Sweden was named the <a href="/wiki/List_of_IIHF_World_Championship_directorate_award_winners" title="List of IIHF World Championship directorate award winners">tournament's most valuable player as well as top goaltender</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <b>2011 IIHF World Championship rosters</b> consisted of 397 players from 16 national ice hockey teams. Organised by the <a href="/wiki/International_Ice_Hockey_Federation" title="International Ice Hockey Federation">International Ice Hockey Federation</a> (IIHF), the 2011 IIHF World Championship, held in <a href="/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">Bratislava</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ko%C5%A1ice" title="Košice">Košice</a>, Slovakia, was the 75th edition of the tournament. <a href="/wiki/Finland_men%27s_national_ice_hockey_team" title="Finland men's national ice hockey team">Finland</a> won the tournament for the second time defeating <a href="/wiki/Sweden_men%27s_national_ice_hockey_team" title="Sweden men's national ice hockey team">Sweden</a> 6–1 in the final.<sup id="cite_ref-MEDALTABLE_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MEDALTABLE-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FINLANDWIN_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FINLANDWIN-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>Before the start of the tournament, each participating nation had to submit a list of players for its roster. A minimum of 15 skaters and two <a href="/wiki/Goaltender" title="Goaltender">goaltenders</a> and a maximum of 20 skaters and three goaltenders had to be selected. After the start of the tournament, each team was allowed to add additional players to their roster, for a maximum of 25. Once players were registered to the team, they could not be removed from the roster.<sup id="cite_ref-PLAYERENTRY_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PLAYERENTRY-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>To have qualified for the national team under IIHF rules, a player must have met several criteria. He must be a citizen of the nation, and be under the jurisdiction of that national association. Players are allowed to change which national team they represent, providing they fulfill the IIHF criteria. If participating for the first time in an IIHF event, the player was required to have played two consecutive years in the national competition of the new country without playing in another country. If the player has already played for a national team before, he may switch countries if he is a citizen of the new country, and has played for four consecutive years in the national competition of the new country. This switch may happen only once in the player's life.<sup id="cite_ref-ELIGIBILITY_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ELIGIBILITY-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Viktor_Fasth" title="Viktor Fasth">Viktor Fasth</a> of Sweden was named the <a href="/wiki/List_of_IIHF_World_Championship_directorate_award_winners" title="List of IIHF World Championship directorate award winners">tournament's most valuable player</a> and top goaltender by the IIHF directorate.<sup id="cite_ref-MEDIAALLSTARS_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MEDIAALLSTARS-5">[5]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BESTPLAYERS_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BESTPLAYERS-6">[6]</a></sup> Canadian <a href="/wiki/Alex_Pietrangelo" title="Alex Pietrangelo">Alex Pietrangelo</a> was named the top <a href="/wiki/Defenceman" title="Defenceman">defenceman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jarom%C3%ADr_J%C3%A1gr" title="Jaromír Jágr">Jaromír Jágr</a> of the Czech Republic was selected as the top <a href="/wiki/Forward_(ice_hockey)" title="Forward (ice hockey)">forward</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BESTPLAYERS_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BESTPLAYERS-6">[6]</a></sup> Finland's <a href="/wiki/Jarkko_Immonen" title="Jarkko Immonen">Jarkko Immonen</a> was the tournament's leading scorer with 12 points and <a href="/wiki/Petri_Vehanen" title="Petri Vehanen">Petri Vehanen</a> was the leading goaltender with a <a href="/wiki/Save_percentage" title="Save percentage">save percentage</a> of 0.954.<sup id="cite_ref-LEADINGSCORER_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEADINGSCORER-7">[7]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LEADINGGOALIE_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEADINGGOALIE-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<p><br /></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Canada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Head coach</b>: <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/23px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/35px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/46px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Ken_Hitchcock" title="Ken Hitchcock">Ken Hitchcock</a>&#160;<span style="font-size:90%;">(<abbr title="Canada">CAN</abbr>)</span></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skaters_3">Skaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Skaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG" class="image"><img alt="An ice hockey player leaning forward on his ice hockey stick and facing to the left of the camera. He is wearing a black helmet and uniform." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG/200px-AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG" width="200" height="276" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG/300px-AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG/400px-AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2042" data-file-height="2818" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:AlexPietrangeloCanada.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Czech Republic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Head coach</b>: <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Czech_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Alois_Hadamczik" title="Alois Hadamczik">Alois Hadamczik</a>&#160;<span style="font-size:90%;">(<abbr title="Czech Republic">CZE</abbr>)</span></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skaters_4">Skaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Skaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<ul>
<li><b>Head coach</b>: <span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/23px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/35px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/46px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Glen_Hanlon" title="Glen Hanlon">Glen Hanlon</a>&#160;<span style="font-size:90%;">(<abbr title="Canada">CAN</abbr>)</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skaters_12">Skaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Skaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Satan_Bruins.jpg" class="image"><img alt="An ice hockey player standing, facing towards the camera. He is wearing a black helmet and a black, yellow and white uniform." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Satan_Bruins.jpg/200px-Satan_Bruins.jpg" width="200" height="235" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Satan_Bruins.jpg/300px-Satan_Bruins.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Satan_Bruins.jpg/400px-Satan_Bruins.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1077" data-file-height="1263" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Satan_Bruins.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Miroslav_%C5%A0atan" title="Miroslav Šatan">Miroslav Šatan</a> played six games, recording three goals and two assists, tying for first amongst his team in scoring.</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovenia">Slovenia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Slovenia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skaters_14">Skaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Skaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG" class="image"><img alt="An ice hockey player standing, facing towards the camera. He is wearing a blue helmet and a blue and yellow uniform." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG/200px-MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG" width="200" height="298" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG/300px-MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG/400px-MagnusPaajarviSvensson.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1154" data-file-height="1722" /></a>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Skaters_16">Skaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2011_IIHF_World_Championship_rosters&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Skaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
